msg:Very nice Hotel, close to the beach in Yingkou. Great location, great view to the Harbor and to the beach.

This weekend was fully booked which showed some disappointments:
- the kitchen staff and restaurant service personal was completely overwhelmed
- the breakfast area was very crowded and very noise

Unfortunately also the cleaning staff was very busy. Cigarettes leftovers in the room or on the floors were not wiped away. 

Also outside the Hotel the area full of entertainment: fireworks till late night, beach parties with karaoke sessions long after midnight. Sleeping nearly impossible. During daytime one of the most interesting activities was the Helicopter flight, every 5min 2 flybys next to the hotel kept the noise level very.
